Germany Actively Prepares for War - Secretly Establishes Airfields Across the Country - Ambition to Advance Eastward is Obvious - A Famous French Reporter Publishes an Article

(Paris) The famous French reporter, Lucien, who is familiar with the situation of Germany's military preparations, has recently written an article commenting on Germany's war preparations and secretly setting up airfields. This article will be published in the Mariana Weekly, which will be published tomorrow. The article cites the British White Paper on National Defense, the facts discovered by Stett, the editor-in-chief of The Times, and the German military requirements published by the "Little Parisian Newspaper" 18 months ago. In addition, most of the materials were provided by Mrs. Woodman of England. Mrs. Woodman is the secretary of the British Democratic Supervision Association and is a well-known expert in military affairs. Lucien's article briefly states that according to various statistics, Germany has 62 airfields, but according to official documents, Germany actually has 258 airfields, and this number is the minimum, because the 2,500 German aviation sports organizations have opened many airfields. In addition, there are sports grounds and racecourses everywhere that can be used for landing aircraft, and all lakes can be used for landing seaplanes. Most of the recently built airfields have factories, barracks, and underground hangars. Sixteen aircraft can take off simultaneously from the rotating airfield. Most of these airfields are built in forests far from cities and are concealed and kept secret. In addition, Lucien also listed the names of German flying squadron officers. As for the German aircraft's attack bases, those set up in the Cologne area and Münster, Hanover, and Kiel are for attacking the United Kingdom. Those set up in Cologne, Darmstadt, Sengcheng, and Nuremberg are for attacking France. If Italy is attacked from Bavaria or Württemberg, it can be reached in a few hours, because the distance from Sengcheng to Rome is only 700 kilometers, and the distance from Sengcheng to Trieste, Italy, is only 320 kilometers, and it takes less than an hour to fly from Sengcheng to northern Italy. In addition, the Czech Republic is surrounded by the air force in Upper Silesia, Saxony, and Bavaria. Although Germany and Poland have good relations, Germany has built many airfields in East Prussia, which is absolutely unnecessary in terms of civil transportation. The threat to the Baltic countries is even worse, because the defense capabilities of the Baltic countries are very weak and can be invaded at any time. However, the main purpose of Germany's aerial invasion is the Soviet Union, which can be seen from the fact that German airfields are moving towards the eastern border. (Havas Telegram on the 23rd)

(Paris) A well-known stockbroker in London recently told the Economic and Financial Communications Agency that Germany has a large amount of money stored abroad for war, at least 500 million pounds, mostly stored in Amsterdam, Netherlands, Switzerland, and the United States, specifically for the purchase of raw materials and the funds to implement rearmament. German Minister of Economy Dr. Schacht has repeatedly declared to the outside world that Germany lacks current currency, using this as an excuse to default on debts. This is nothing more than a way to delay time so as to complete the plan to strengthen the military and prepare for war. The broker also said that he still remembers that in 1923, the German banks in South America, Brazil, Uruguay, Argentina, and Chile entrusted him to sell a large number of marks. At that time, the credit of German currency in the commercial market had not fallen, so there was no worry about finding a buyer. The estimated amount of the transaction was about 100 million pounds. This huge amount was immediately transferred to the German authorities and secretly stored in a safe place under a pseudonym. (Havas Telegram on the 23rd)

Defensive Mutual Assistance Pact: French-Russian Negotiations Stalled, French Experts Study Solutions to Difficulties, Avoiding Conflicts with Britain and Italy

(Paris) According to sources here, the Soviet Russian government gazette stated that Foreign Affairs Commissar Litvinov's negotiations with French Foreign Minister Laval had been temporarily suspended. Litvinov had returned to Moscow to report everything to the People's Committee. News of this surprised various circles in France, as the gazette did not mention when the negotiations would resume. Furthermore, according to French authorities, the negotiations naturally ceased when Litvinov returned to the Russian capital. It is noted that Litvinov and Laval had resolved the main points in their previous talks, and only a few points in the articles remained unresolved when Litvinov departed. According to a French gazette, Litvinov wanted to report to the Soviet Russian People's Committee, and Laval would also report to the French cabinet. However, opinions differed more in the Soviet Russian side than in France. (National Telegraph, 23rd)

(Paris) Difficulties have arisen in the proposed Franco-Russian defensive mutual assistance pact, causing negotiations to temporarily stall. Today, French legal experts are meeting to study ways to eliminate these difficulties. French diplomats are keen to preserve the original intention of the Franco-Russian agreement while avoiding conflicts with Britain and France. According to the draft agreement, if either Russia or France is subjected to any aggression by another country, they will implement military mutual assistance. Therefore, the proposed formal treaty is broader in scope than the air defense mutual assistance pact advocated by British Foreign Secretary Simon. The French side intends to sign this agreement before the opening of the Rome conference in mid-May, and an agreement with Czechoslovakia is also planned. However, it is heard that Britain and Italy may oppose such separately signed military alliances, hindering France's plan. (National Telegraph, 23rd)

(Moscow) Soviet Russian officials today remained silent regarding the temporary suspension of Franco-Russian military agreement negotiations. However, Soviet Russian newspapers prominently published dispatches from Paris stating that the reason for the temporary suspension was that France felt it necessary to submit the agreement to the League of Nations for final approval. Soviet Russian officials believed that the sooner the agreement was signed, the better. Since returning from Geneva, Soviet Russian Foreign Affairs Commissar Litvinov has neither confirmed nor denied the current state of affairs regarding this matter. (National Telegraph, 23rd)

(Paris) Newspapers have rarely commented on the temporary suspension of Franco-Russian mutual assistance pact negotiations. The right-wing newspaper "White Day" expressed no dissatisfaction with the matter, stating, "According to the news released by TASS, the Franco-Russian negotiations have now been temporarily suspended. This is precisely the opportunity we desire, as we must have considerable time to consider what Russia is requesting." The newspaper "Free Man" stated, "Between France and Russia lie Germany and Poland. Any words or actions between France and Russia must take Germany and Poland into account. The reason why the Franco-Russian mutual assistance pact has been delayed is likely because the two countries have not fully considered Germany and Poland. Even if the pact is completed, what value does it have if Poland obstructs its implementation?" The "Paris Echo" stated that if France wants to conclude a security pact, then it is necessary to sign a mutual assistance pact with the Soviet Union. As long as this pact is not concluded, the Little Entente countries will not agree to negotiate the Danube Pact. A reporter from the "Little Parisian" newspaper in Moscow stated, "Except for a small number of foreigners, no one believes in the breakdown of Franco-Russian negotiations. Although officials in the Soviet Union remain secretive, they only say that the suspension of talks is temporary. As for the Franco-Russian cooperation policy, it will definitely not be affected."

French Renowned Reporter Criticizes Laval's Diplomacy: The Unity of Three Nations Has Not Become a Powerful Tool, Hesitation and Indecisiveness Have Led to a Loss of Essential Authority

(Paris) Morning News reporter Botinard strongly criticized French policy after the Stresa and Geneva conferences, stating that the results of the Stresa conference proved that the unity of Britain, France, and Italy had failed to become a powerful tool. Britain still intends to refuse to bear responsibility for the European continent. At the end of January, the British Foreign Office planned to restore the pre-war Entente, but due to opposition from overseas territories, domestic public opinion, and other cabinet members, Prime Minister MacDonald and Foreign Secretary Simon may have been prepared to reaffirm the obligations of the Locarno Treaty. However, the treaty itself has become a dead letter after several changes, and the League of Nations has failed to stop minor aggressions. British Chancellor of the Exchequer Chamberlain stated last month that the League of Nations can only stop wars when great powers do not need wars. Therefore, the only thing that can be done today is for France, Russia, Russia, Czechoslovakia, France, and Italy to separately conclude mutual assistance pacts. However, the most important Franco-Russian pact has now suffered a setback. Foreign Minister Laval's hesitation and indecisiveness have led to a loss of his essential authority. Now, only direct talks between Mussolini of Italy, Benes of Czechoslovakia, Titulescu of Romania, and Yevtic of Yugoslavia can preserve the Danube conference. (National News Agency, 23rd)

French Troops Concentrated on the German Border

(Paris) Dozens of special trains filled with thousands of new recruits departed for the vicinity of the Rhine River today. This is part of the French Ministry of the Army's concentration plan. These new recruits are draftees who enlisted after the French cabinet passed the new conscription law, numbering between 115,000 and 120,000. Most of them will undergo one year of rigorous military training, but in the event of an emergency, their term of military service will be automatically extended. (National Telegraph, 23rd)

Polish Government Newspaper Denies Secret German-Polish Agreement

Warsaw: Foreign sources have reported that Poland has entered into a secret agreement with Germany. The French newspapers "Paris Echo" and "Lyon National Welfare" have disclosed the details of the agreement. The government-affiliated "Daily Express" has once again denied this, stating, "Such news should be regarded as a deliberate attempt aimed at creating an atmosphere in Western Europe unfavorable to Poland." (Havas, 23rd)

Threatened by Germany, Lithuania Prepares its Military, Army Strength Increased to 20,000

Lithuanian Capital: The Lithuanian government is currently increasing its army's armaments and troop numbers in order to cope with Germany's rearmament in East Prussia. To date, only one-third of Lithuanian conscripts have been enlisted for service. The government has now decided to form the remaining one-third and other reservists into special divisions. Furthermore, the government recently decided to retain soldiers who were due to be discharged, keeping them in service. As a result, the Lithuanian standing army can be increased from 14,000 to 20,000. Including reservists, the total reaches 31,000. Various defensive weapons, such as anti-tank guns and anti-aircraft guns, will be improved. (Havas, 23rd)

Page 7

British Newspapers Not Surprised by German Disregard for League of Nations Resolution, Believe International Negotiations Are Still Open

(London) Since the German government's protest against the League of Nations condemnation resolution was delivered to Britain, there has been no alarm in British public opinion. Most newspapers believe that the wording of the German dispatch is very mild, given the tense situation. The Times stated that Germany feels most dissatisfied with the League of Nations, not with any single country. As for Germany's eventual return to Geneva, it has suffered a significant blow. However, the possibility of collective action still seems to exist. The Daily Telegraph stated that, as things stand, it cannot be said that Germany has cut off the path of negotiations with Western European countries. It has been learned from Moscow that Franco-Russian negotiations have now been declared broken. Germany's attitude may soften somewhat upon hearing this. The Sunday Times stated that Germany's annoyance was expected, and the major powers should have foreseen it. The Observer's reporter Garvin stated that the joint protest issued at the end of the Stresa conference was sufficient in terms of quality and seriousness, and there was no need to take other steps. In the abstract, the Geneva resolution is undoubtedly correct, but in practical politics, it is meaningless. (National Telegraph, 22nd)

German Dispatch Delivered to Moscow

(Moscow) It was announced here today that the Foreign Ministry received Germany's formal note protesting the League of Nations' condemnation of its violation of the Treaty of Versailles on the 20th. Official sources and Soviet Russian newspapers did not comment at all on Germany's

Who is the Culprit of the European War? Former Austro-Hungarian Prime Minister Tries to Exonerate Himself

(Vienna) Some people accuse former Austro-Hungarian Prime Minister Berchtold of being one of the culprits of the European War. Berchtold recently gave an interview to the "Sunday Monday Newspaper," denying this claim. He said that the reason why Austria-Hungary decided to declare war on Serbia in 1914 was because Germany encouraged it. At that time, German Ambassador to Austria Tschirschky advised Emperor William II not to urge Austria so fervently. William II replied, "Who allowed Tschirschky to take such an attitude? In the future, we can say that Germany did not want war." (Havas, 23rd)

Chairman of the Disarmament Conference Discusses the International Situation: The Far East Incident Caused Countries to Expand Militaries, Britain Will Be Drawn into the Vortex if a Great War Breaks Out, Germany's Return to the League of Nations is an Element of European Peace

(London) Chairman of the Disarmament Conference Henderson recently gave a speech in Scarborough, stating, "The arms race that countries are now engaged in is largely due to the Far East Incident. There are two centers of global turmoil: one in the Far East and one in Europe. However, peace is a whole and cannot be divided. If we want to divide the responsibility for maintaining peace and not cooperate with each other, the result will only be to invalidate the League of Nations Covenant, and the door to a second European war will be opened. If a second world war breaks out, Britain will inevitably be drawn into the vortex. Therefore, within the scope of a general security system, the success or failure of resolving the issue of Germany's arms equality is extremely important. We believe that Germany's return to Geneva and its full acceptance of the various obligations in the League of Nations Covenant are indispensable elements for truly resolving international problems, and it is for this reason." (Havas, 22nd)

Italy Encourages Marriage: 2,000 Newlywed Couples, Government Subsidies for Honeymoons

(Rome) Italy has become a honeymoon country today, as more than 2,000 newlywed couples are having their expenses paid by the Fascist Party to enjoy their holidays. Newlywed couples who marry on Easter Monday can receive 500 lire each. This is part of the government's marriage encouragement plan. (National News Agency, 23rd)

Bulgarian New Cabinet's Foreign Policy: Enhance Friendship with Yugoslavia, Decide to Draft a New Constitution

Sofia: The tense political situation in Bulgaria, with the risk of civil war breaking out at any time, has stabilized since King Boris appointed Touchiev to form a cabinet last Friday. Touchiev served as the ambassador to Serbia during the First Balkan War and as the ambassador to Turkey after the Second Balkan War. Therefore, he is very familiar with the Balkan issue. New Foreign Minister Kosev has also recently served as the ambassador to Yugoslavia. New Prime Minister Touchiev told reporters that all members of the new government are determined to implement the policy of May 19 last year. The new government has the king's trust. The king of Bulgaria's power, which had been greatly reduced by the previous two governments, has now been fully restored. Soldiers occupy only three seats in the new government, and the new Minister of the Army, Ninav, is known for opposing military interference in politics, proving that the military warlords cannot control the political situation. As for foreign policy, there will be no major changes. Touchiev recently stated that he cannot tolerate the arrogance of the Macedonian faction and is determined to enhance friendly relations with Yugoslavia. The new cabinet held its first meeting today, appointing the Prime Minister and Minister of Justice to draft a constitutional reform plan. (National Telegraph, 23rd)

Yugoslav Capital: The political turmoil in Bulgaria was resolved successfully a few days ago. People here were very satisfied to hear the news, because both the new Prime Minister Touchiev and Foreign Minister Kosev have served as diplomatic envoys and have been stationed in Yugoslavia for a long time. Their friendship with Yugoslavia is well-known. Touchiev told reporters from the Avala News Agency that the new government's domestic and foreign policies will remain the same, adhering to the spirit of the May 19, 1934 coup. It will maintain good friendship with all neighboring countries, and especially with Yugoslavia, it will be sincere and closely cooperative. This is for "the common welfare of the two countries, as well as for the benefit of peace." Foreign Minister Kosev also issued his first declaration to the Avala News Agency, stating that he will strive to closely cooperate with Yugoslavia. This policy is not only endorsed by the entire government, but also supported by the entire Bulgarian people. (Havas, 23rd)

International Commercial Telegrams — April 23, Reuters Special Commercial News Telegram —

Gold and Silver

London Gold Price: Today is 243 shillings and 6 pence, down 1 pence. The London bullion market is very firm, with the spot price at 32 pence and 375, and the futures price at 32 pence and a half, both up 1 pence and 4375. The rise in silver prices is mostly due to speculative trading, and there are not many sellers. The closing market is uncertain.

Exchange Rates

British-American: The London foreign exchange market was very quiet today, with very little price fluctuation. The opening exchange rate for British-American was 4 dollars, 8 dimes, and 5 cents, the same as the closing exchange rate for British-American on Saturday and Sunday. The price fell 3125 in the first hour to 4 dollars, 8 dimes, 4 cents, and 6875. It rebounded 125 at noon to 4 dollars, 8 dimes, 4 cents, and 8125. There were no further changes after this price. The opening rate for British-French was unchanged, remaining at 73 francs and 59. It fell 5 pounds at 11 o'clock and rebounded 3 pounds at noon, to 73 francs and 57. This price remained unchanged until the time of transmission.

Rubber

London: The rubber market was stable today. The trading price for July-September futures at noon was 5 pence and 875, up 0625 from the previous closing. The New York rubber market opened lower due to a lack of exciting news. The price rebounded slightly as the market became more active.

Cotton and Wheat

American Cotton: The New York cotton market opened today with slightly lower prices due to unsettled weather. The price rebounded as buying activity and news from Liverpool were also good. There is talk that the footing is stronger than before.

American Wheat: The Chicago wheat market tended to loosen today. The market opened with a slight drop, and prices seemed to continue to fall due to news of good wheat production conditions.

British Wheat: The Liverpool wheat market was stable this morning. The price for the July-August period was 5 shillings and 9 pence at 1 p.m., up half a penny.

British Cotton: The Liverpool cotton market was also stable today. The July period rose 5 pounds at 1 p.m. to 6.36.

New York: The stock exchange opened this morning and the market remained stable. Trading was quite active, and most stocks rose, especially mining stocks and oil stocks. Tragedy in Chicago: Bank Employee Has a Nervous Breakdown and Shoots His Own Children to Death

Chicago: A tragedy that Ibsen and Werner could not have imagined has occurred here in a middle-class family. A bank employee named Gardner had a nervous breakdown before dawn today, shooting and killing his 20-year-old beautiful daughter Rita and 14-year-old son Donna, and wounding his 17-year-old son Ghana. His wife was fortunate to escape unharmed. After Gardner was taken into custody, he declared, "I want to eradicate the mental illness in my family. I was going to wipe everyone out, then commit suicide." This man is short, looks like a frightened rabbit, and does not resemble a murderer. He said that he and his wife had suffered from tuberculosis and that his head "always felt strange." He heard that his children were also complaining, saying that they felt uneasy in their heads. So they roamed around all night, plotting to solve everything. Before dawn, he finally made up his mind, took out a pistol and began to eliminate the whole family. After several shots, the whole family was shocked and called the police. The tragedy was only half-finished, but it was too inhumane. (National Telegraph, 22nd)

Butcher Invents a New Type of Boat: Using a Water Pump to Propel the Hull, the Speed Can Reach 20 Kilometers per Hour

(Paris) A butcher in Dourdan, named Menard, has invented a new type of boat that has no oars, no sails, and no propulsion engine. The speed can reach 20 kilometers per hour. The method is to install a water pump inside the boat, which is powered by an engine. The pump draws water from the bow of the boat, causing the hull to slide forward, and then discharges water from the stern, agitating the waves to propel the hull forward. The manufacturing method is very ingenious. (Havas, 22nd)

Legal Rights Research Association to be Established

(Nanjing) The Legal Rights Research Association will be established next month. There will be fourteen members, one appointed by the Central Government, one appointed by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, two appointed by the Judicial Yuan, seven elected by the Ministry, and three legal experts from various regions will be hired as members. Hong Ludong is appointed as the chairman, and Xie Jian is proposed as the deputy chairman. The first phase will study the experiences of Japan, Turkey, and other countries in revitalizing and recovering legal rights. (Special Dispatch, 23rd)

(Nanjing) Representatives of various groups in Jiangxi, including Wang Mingxuan, went to the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Finance on the afternoon of the 23rd to request subsidies for security expenses. Postal Bureau's Financial Transactions to be Primarily Through the Central Bank of China

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Finance forwarded a request from the Central Bank to the Ministry of Communications' Postal Savings and Remittances Bureau, stating that bank financial transactions should be primarily through the Central Bank of China. Payments should be made exclusively with Central Bank banknotes. The Ministry of Communications replied that the postal bureau had complied with the request. All previously used marked notes from other banks have now expired and have been discontinued and will not be renewed. (Special Dispatch, 23rd)

(Nanjing) Zhang Fang, Chairman of the Henan Relief Committee, submitted a report to the Executive Yuan, stating that after the completion of the breakwater closure and confluence project, the floodwaters in the disaster-stricken counties and districts in Huaifeng are gradually receding. (Nanjing) Since the Anhui Provincial Government increased the tea tax this year, the Anhui Association in Shanghai has telegraphed the Ministry of Finance, requesting that the Ministry instruct the Anhui Provincial Government to abolish the increased tea tax and continue to collect taxes according to the actual tea prices of the current year. The Ministry of Finance transferred the request to the competent department for review. (Special Dispatch, 23rd)

Ministry of Finance Revises Regulations on Tobacco and Alcohol License Tax

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Finance recently revised and promulgated the regulations on tobacco and alcohol license tax. Except for the Class B wholesale of foreign liquor, which is set at 15 yuan per quarter, the rest remain the same. The Ministry of Finance also telegraphed the provincial and municipal governments, requesting them to exchange the old licenses for the Ministry-issued Class B wholesale licenses for foreign liquor. The Ministry of Industry Requests Interpretation of Commercial Clauses

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Industry requested an interpretation from the Judicial Yuan regarding the question of whether foreigners can serve as shareholders, directors, or supervisors of Chinese companies. The Judicial Yuan has interpreted that foreigners may serve as shareholders, directors, or supervisors of Chinese companies, provided that the company's articles of association and current laws and regulations contain no restrictions. Central Agricultural Experiment Station Sends Personnel to Investigate Rice Stem Borer Conditions in Various Provinces

(Nanjing) The Central Agricultural Experiment Station previously sent Technician Yang Banghua and others to various provinces in the upper reaches of the Yangtze River to investigate the overwintering conditions of rice stem borers. Yang and others have now investigated along the route from Nanjing to Hunan. According to the survey results, rice stem borers are very numerous in various locations in Hunan and Hubei, and the distribution of rice stem borers is also extremely common along the Yangtze River. Currently, Mr. Yang and his party are still conducting investigations separately in Hubei and Jiangxi. (Central News Agency dispatch from the 23rd)

Bandits Throw Bombs into Restaurants After Extortion Fails

(Guangzhou) Bandits in Guangzhou have repeatedly extorted money from tea houses and restaurants. Because the Heji Restaurant did not comply with their demands, they threw a bomb into the restaurant last night when it was full of diners. One waiter had his arm blown off, and the customers all fled in panic. The neighbors were greatly shocked. The authorities immediately imposed martial law and searched for the bandits. It is reported that two people have been arrested. The injured person was immediately sent to the hospital, and it is reported that his injuries are quite serious. (Reuters dispatch from the 22nd)

Huaiyin and Surrounding Areas Designated as Suppression Zones

Huaiyin: After the establishment of the Seventh District Provisional Command Headquarters in Huaiyin on the 15th, mobilization began immediately. All county magistrates and military and political personnel in the district also worked with the army. It is learned that Commander Wang Depu divided the area into three suppression zones at the time: the first zone was the northern part of Suqian and Siyang, the second zone was the southern part of Huaiyin and Siyang, and the third zone was the entire LianShui. In the past week, approximately 200 bandits and accomplices have been captured and are being investigated separately. Mr. Wang himself is also preparing to set off to personally supervise the various districts, and the situation is very tense. (Special dispatch from the 23rd)

Deng Jiayan Passes Through Xuzhou on His Return to Beijing

(Xuzhou) Deng Jiayan, a special envoy of the National Government to pay tribute to the Yellow Emperor's Mausoleum, arrived in Xuzhou on the morning of the 23rd with his wife from Shaanxi and took the evening train to Beijing. Ministry of Railways Investigation Team Passes Through Xuzhou

(Xuzhou) In order to complete the extension of the entire Longhai Railway to Lanzhou, the Ministry of Railways has specially dispatched an economic investigation team to investigate the economic, agricultural, and mineral conditions along the Xi'an-Lanzhou line to provide a reference for the construction of the road. It is reported that specialists Lin Yingyun, Li Liangkun, Luo Mingshu, Zhang Jiajie, Liu Binglun, and Lu Yanbiao, among others, arrived in Xuzhou on the morning of the 23rd and went west via Zhengzhou at noon, meeting with Qian Zongze. The Longhai Railway Bureau specially dispatched two people to accompany them. The team is divided into two lines, one going from Xi'an through Changwu to Lanzhou, and the other going from Xi'an through Baoji to Lanzhou, each responsible for investigating more than 20 counties. It is expected to be completed and returned to Beijing in June. After the Ministry of Railways receives the team's report, it will begin to extend the Xi'an-Lanzhou Railway. It is reported that the northern line is planned for track laying because an automotive highway is already under construction on the southern line. (Central News Agency dispatch from the 23rd)

A Perspective on the Italo-Ethiopian Dispute

— (Rome Correspondence)

From one perspective, Italy's national strength can be said to be thriving, with a tendency to compete with Germany and France. However, its domestic production is very small, especially for the materials necessary for modern industrial countries—coal, iron, oil, etc. Therefore, on the other hand, with the development of its national strength, the number of unemployed people has increased from 200,000 to more than a million, and foreign trade is also in a difficult position. Therefore, Italy must seek a way out, on the one hand, to open up new colonies overseas, and on the other hand, to control the contradictions within the country. Coincidentally, on November 23rd of last year, a military conflict occurred between Italian and Ethiopian border troops near the Ualual and Wardir wells. Since this incident, Italy, on the one hand, has wanted to show the authority of a great power, and on the other hand, it wants to take this opportunity to display its skills, in other words, to stimulate its domestic industry.

For example, in recent years, world trade has declined, and Italian merchant ships sailing in the Atlantic Ocean have also suffered from suspensions. Since the Italo-Ethiopian dispute, those suspended ships have all been mobilized as transport ships for the expeditionary force. All unemployed crew members have been reinstated. Various military supply manufacturing factories, or factories related to military supplies, have suddenly become active and are operating day and night. Automobile factories and aircraft factories are swamped with orders. The Italian government is also preparing for total mobilization. If Abyssinia really wants to resist, Italy really seems to be going all out to fight her. But what about Abyssinia? Although Abyssinia is a small independent African country, its area is only 350,000 square miles, and its population is only over seven million (some estimate it to be ten million). The total length of the national railway is only 487 miles. However, there are as many as two million people who can charge into battle. Although they do not have modern weapons, their national character is extremely brave and unyielding. Moreover, King Haile Selassi, although expressing his willingness to resolve the Italo-Ethiopian conflict peacefully, does not relax his military preparations. When the Italian army mobilized to East Africa, the King of Abyssinia also issued a national mobilization order, and he himself announced that he would be the commander-in-chief, with the crown prince as the military supervisor, using the greatest spirit of sacrifice to maintain his country. Italy cannot help but be somewhat wary of this, so it accepted peace, advocated listening to the arbitration of the League of Nations, and did not immediately declare war.

However, there is another reason for not declaring war immediately, which is the complex relationship between Britain, France, and Italy. Because on December 13, 1906, Britain, France, and Italy reached the following secret understanding on the Abyssinian question: (1) Abyssinia is within the sphere of influence of Britain, France, and Italy; (2) the territorial integrity of Abyssinia; (3) the three countries jointly protect each other's interests and maintain equal opportunities. In 1919, Britain, in order to develop the water conservancy of Lake Tana, recognized Italy's right to build a longitudinal railway from Italian Somaliland to Abyssinia, preferential commercial rights along the railway, and other economic rights. In the Rome Agreement of January 7 this year, France also agreed to transfer two or three thousand shares of the Franco-Ethiopian Railway to Italy. Based on this, it seems that Britain, France, and Italy can understand each other, but what they understand is "equal opportunity," not that any one country can occupy it alone.

Now, Italy's attempt is to conquer Abyssinia by force. If it is to attack by railway, it must have the consent of France, and even the understanding of Britain. Even if it occupies "Addis Ababa" (the capital of Abyssinia), it cannot be considered completely resolved. Moreover, it is not easy for the Italian army, with its modern organization, to engage in purely manual labor and horsepower movements in mountainous terrain, and to engage in scattered field battles with the brave Ethiopian cavalry. Therefore, although Italy uses intimidating methods to make Abyssinia submit, it can also stimulate Italy's own industry. Although the atmosphere of war is strong, it is not necessarily realized. (March 24, Rome)

Since the Northeast Exchange Began, Inward Remittances from Beyond the Customs Have Gradually Increased. In February and March, Inward Remittances Were Less Than 300,000 Yuan, Mostly from Shandong and Hebei Provinces, Followed by Shanghai and Hankou

Tianjin Correspondence: Since the restoration of Northeast exchange on February 1st of this year, remittances have shown a declining trend. Recently, the Japanese and puppet regimes have implemented regulations restricting Chinese laborers from leaving the customs, which has further affected remittances. In order to understand the actual situation, the reporter inquired at the remittance office of the General Bureau of Postal Savings Industry on Fourth Malu. According to Director Fang of the office, inward remittances from beyond the customs in February reached more than 20,000 yuan, and in March, it was more than 200,000 yuan. Among them, remittances to Shandong, Hebei, Shanxi, and Anhui provinces were the most, followed by Shanghai and Hankou. Outward remittances from the mainland were more than 10,000 yuan in February and more than 20,000 yuan in March, all remitted to Changchun, Heilongjiang, and other places. However, in total, inward remittances from the Northeast in these two months were less than 300,000 yuan, a decrease of nearly two-thirds compared to the past monthly inward remittances of 800,000 to 900,000 yuan. However, inward remittances in April reached more than 200,000 yuan, indicating an improvement in the situation in fact. The economic relationship between the compatriots in the Northeast under subjugation and the mainland, after years of obstruction, has only begun to show this phenomenon today. However, with Japan's invasion of China still unfinished, the future is still unknown. (Northeast News Agency)

Guantai Confluence Construction Process: No More Water Accumulation at the Changyuan City Walls

Nanjing Correspondence: Since the Central Government ordered the Shanxi-Henan Disaster Relief Committee's Works and Relief Group to take charge of the Guantai Yellow River confluence project, the group has actively proceeded. On the 11th of this month, the 29-meter-deep breach was successfully closed, and the news was celebrated throughout the country. Various details have been repeatedly recorded in this newspaper. The Water Conservancy Committee of the Economic Council, based on a report submitted by Kong Xiangrong, Director of the Works and Relief Group, regarding the Guantai confluence construction process, has made valuable research on river works. The details are specially explored as follows: (Above omitted) According to the report submitted by the Engineering Section of the group, the Guantai breach is located at the bend of the Yellow River channel, where the river divides into two branches: one is a diversion at the bend, and the other is a backflow due to the obstruction angle downstream. The backflow is more violent, so the eastern headland is constantly scoured. Since March 21st, efforts have been made to protect it, but the costs have been high. On the evening of the 26th, the peach blossom flood came down, and the flow was as fierce as rushing cattle, constantly surging. Fortunately, the situation was stabilized after all-night rescue efforts and thorough preparations. However, the river's branched entrance remained the same. With such a large flow in front of us, and the depth of the breach being about 29 meters, it was difficult to start closing the breach. It was not possible to succeed without quickly guiding the river flow into the middle channel and reducing the flow's scouring force. Therefore, on the 27th, we began to build two permeable willow dams upstream. The first dam was 175 meters long, and the second dam was 207 meters long. By April 5th, they were completed one after another. However, the willow dams were permeable in nature, and their ends were difficult to intersect smoothly with the upstream protruding angle, so although the flow was slightly dispersed, it was still close at the beginning and farther apart later. The harm of the backflow could not be completely eliminated. The breach closing project was implemented on the 6th, but the effect was minimal. Therefore, on the 7th, we arranged civilian ships and densely dropped anchored ropes to form a floating dam, which formed a T-shaped right angle with the middle channel, starting from the corner of the western dam and ending at the edge of the middle channel. At that time, the middle flow was finally brought under control and flowed straight down, and its function was the same as that of the permeable willow dam. From then on, the branched flows were gradually cut off, and the breach closing project was intensified and progressed vigorously. Layer by layer, willow skin and stone pillows, about half a meter in diameter and 13 meters long, were sunk. On the 7th, the breach was raised by more than four meters. On the 8th and 9th, a total of 529 bundles of pillows were sunk, raising it more than five meters above the original branch riverbed. As a result, the water势 in the breach was almost like water flowing from a ditch, only overflowing from the gaps. On the 10th, the water depth of the breach was measured to be only three meters. Therefore, we worked hard to consolidate it and filled the gaps with pillows. By the morning of the 11th, only a breach of about one meter wide and one meter deep remained. With the supervision of the staff, it was blocked and closed in two hours. Willow stones were laid on top of each other, about two meters above the water surface. Then, burlap material and earth bags were used to cover the surface, so that it was as high as the two dams. In the future, earth bags and stones will be added to the outside to thicken the embankment, cultivate the slope, build protective embankments, and then backfill and solidify the soil, so that it can be permanently protected from the turbulent waves and not be affected by the伏汛. Someone said that the speed of this breach closure was mainly due to the function of the permeable willow dam in releasing silt. This argument does not seem to be consistent with the facts and science. The function of the permeable dam is not comparable to the solid force of a stone dam in diverting the flow. Its function can only disperse the flow in the immediate vicinity, and it will converge again at a distance. Moreover, it is difficult to control the flow into the middle channel with its location and strength. If the flow is rapid, the dam body may be difficult to protect, and if the flow is slow, the amount of silt deposited is very small. Therefore, the third floating ship was used as a dam to complete its width. It has been said before that the three dams are only for dispersing the flow and buffering it. If you want to make it actually release silt, it is impossible. The current Yellow River has a velocity of two meters per second, and the sand content is only about two percent, so it is extremely difficult to quickly achieve the effect of releasing silt. It was also found that there was a sloping depression in front of the breach after the confluence, more than ten meters deep, the same as before. The height of this depression is no longer affected by the height of the dam. How can we abandon the near and seek the far, and fill the dam over the depression? The facts are all there and can be pursued, and the principle is as clear as looking in a mirror. In short, the speed of this breach closure was truly due to the rapid preparation experience, transportation, and effective management, as well as the agility of the construction. (Below omitted) After the Guantai confluence, the group sent personnel to the various breaches in the Shiche section, as well as the Taihang Dike and around Changyuan County, to investigate the water level situation. According to the report, the water level in front of Hekou Village on the Taihang Dike has dropped by nine meters since the Guantai confluence. Before the confluence of the Eighth Breach, the original water surface width of the mouth was 164 meters, and now it is 101 meters. The deepest part before was 6.7 meters, and the current depth is 5.8 meters. In the past three days, the water level has dropped by nine meters, and the shallowest part of the mouth is now 2.5 meters. The water surface of the river in front of the Eighth Mouth above the river is now 110 meters wide, and the water depth is 6.5 meters. The water surface behind the river is 17 meters wide and 7 inches deep. It was also found that the original water surface width of the Seventeenth Breach was 178 meters, and now it is 121 meters. The deepest part before was 5.1 meters, and the current depth is 4.2 meters. In the past three days, the water has moved nine inches to the east, and the shallowest part is now 1.2 meters. The water surface of the river in front of the Seventeenth Mouth above the river is 38 meters wide, and the water depth is 4.8 meters. The current water surface behind the river is 26 meters wide and 1.5 meters deep. It was also found that the original depth of the Twenty-First Breach was 9.8 meters, and the current depth is 9 meters. The water surface of the river in front of the mouth above the river is 33 meters wide, and the water depth is 2.8 meters. The surface behind the river is 24 meters wide and 6 inches deep. The water in front of and behind the Twenty-Fifth Breach has receded completely. We also contacted Zhang, the County Magistrate of Changyuan County, and Yang Runzhi, the Vice-Chairman of the City Defense Committee, and reported that this group was ordered to take charge of the Guantai breach repair project, dispatching and transporting, concentrating materials, allocating work, and rushing forward day and night. We took over the job just two weeks ago and were able to announce the confluence. All of this was achieved by following the central government's spirit and comforting the people's long-awaited hopes. According to Vice-Chairman Yang Runzhi, the Director is concerned about the people's suffering and cherishes their difficulties. For the more than 300,000 disaster victims in Changyuan, his kindness is like a second birth. All those who have been rescued are due to the Director's contribution. We admire the Director's arduous efforts and see him as a living Buddha for ten thousand families. We all offer incense and pray for his longevity. His words are sincere and his feelings are pitiful. According to County Magistrate Zhang, the water near the city has dropped by about seven inches in the past three days, and 81 villages that were previously submerged have been evacuated. We then accompanied the County Magistrate, the Vice-Chairman of the City Defense Committee, and representatives from all walks of life to inspect the city walls for a week. There is no longer any accumulated water at the base of the city walls. The drainage ditches and moats in the northwest corner are still flowing. All of this is the situation on the 13th. Now that there is no source of water, it will inevitably dry up day by day. (Central News Agency)

Songjiang: Public Trial of the Quan-Liu Tragic Death Case

The case of Quan Lianfu, a resident of XichiJia Street in Cangqiao, falsely accusing his daughter-in-law Liu of infidelity and instigating his son Quan Wangcai to return home and beat his wife Liu, resulting in serious injuries and death, has been widely rumored. Some rumors say that the father and son beat her to death, while others say that she was beaten and took poison to die. Later, Liu Meichu, the deceased's elder brother, filed a complaint. The procuratorate conducted an investigation and found that the deceased's chest and back were covered with scars, now the color of pig liver, and there were traces of holes from stabbing with a poker, indicating a tragic death. Quan Lianfu and his son Wangcai were prosecuted for homicide, assault, and instigation after interrogation. Quan Wangcai suddenly claimed that his wife had an affair with Zhou Songsheng and was beaten by Zhou's wife when they met on the road. She was ashamed and committed suicide. Zhou was then summoned for interrogation and absolutely denied the allegations, claiming that his wife had died many years ago and insisted that he was being framed. Recently, seven neighbors jointly submitted a petition to the court, requesting lenient punishment, but the petition mentioned that Quan Liu was beaten by Zhou Songsheng's other mistress and committed suicide. Today, Ma Qianru, Yang Xiqing, Zhou Jinchang, and others who signed the joint petition were summoned for questioning. They were asked what evidence they had for the statements in the petition. They all said that the petition was drafted and sent to them by Quan Wangcai's younger brother, Shousheng, for them to stamp, and they did not know the contents. The interrogator then questioned Quan Lianfu about who drafted the petition. Quan Lianfu made all kinds of excuses. After the interrogation, Quan Wangcai was ordered to be returned to custody, awaiting the appointment of a defense lawyer and a scheduled hearing. Quan Lianfu was still handed over to the original guarantor.

Wuxi: Two Men Commit Suicide in Succession

Recently, the trend of suicide has become unstoppable. Statistics show that in the past two months, there have been forty to fifty suicides, both male and female. Unexpectedly, yesterday, two more men committed suicide one after the other. One was Ji Amei, a villager from Huangjia Village near Qingyang Town in Jiangyin, aged thirty. He used to work as a laborer in the Lixin Cloth Factory in this county. However, Huang spent money recklessly, resulting in severe financial difficulties. Recently, he accumulated a large debt that he could not repay. With the idea of suicide in mind, he swallowed two jiao worth of raw opium in the morning. He was discovered by his neighbor and sent to the Brothers Hospital for treatment. Fortunately, the poisoning was not deep, and his life was out of danger. The second was Xu Aquan, a villager from Xi Dafangqiao Village in Anzhen, Eighth District, aged thirty-six. He also had a quarrel with his wife over trivial matters, which was resolved after some persuasion. Aquan left in anger and went to a hotel in the town to drink heavily. After getting drunk, he returned home, grabbed a kitchen knife, and attempted to cut his throat. His wife saw this and rushed him to the Brothers Hospital for treatment. Fortunately, he did not injure his carotid artery or trachea, and his life may be saved.

Our county is implementing the Baojia system, and each district is carrying out the third phase of work, which is nearing completion. The renowned doctor Zhou Mengdan, who lives on Ximen Avenue, is from a family of doctors. His father, Zhou Qitang, was also famous for a time. Mengdan is currently sixty-one years old and has considerable experience in treating external diseases. However, due to years of economic pressure, he has lost over ten thousand yuan. He does not pay much attention to medical affairs and spends his days playing mahjong and drinking yellow wine. On the 21st of this month, he suffered a significant shock and secretly took multiple sleeping pills. He became poisoned in the evening, and doctors on Zhongxi Road were called to perform surgery, but it was ineffective. He died immediately.

Another Famine Fight Erupts in the Sixth District

In the cotton-growing area of the sixth district of this county, which suffered from a severe drought last year, famine riots have repeatedly occurred since winter. Now is the time between the end of one harvest and the beginning of the next, and the starving people in the countryside have nothing to eat but wheat stalks and sweet potatoes. The Disaster Relief Association is about to distribute spring relief, but due to insufficient funds, it has not yet been implemented. However, on the afternoon of the 21st of this month, about one hundred and several tens of old women from the Shuzhou City area gathered at the Lao Wushi District Office, demanding relief from the district chief. The situation was very serious, and many people mistakenly believed that the relief funds had been allocated to the district but were diverted by District Chief Yang for dredging rivers, causing a great uproar that could not be quelled. The local Second District Party Headquarters, together with the district chief, offered earnest persuasion, and they finally dispersed. They have also telegraphed the county government, requesting that relief be released as soon as possible.

His wife, Cai, is thirty-seven years old and has five children. The eldest daughter is eighteen years old, and the second daughter is fourteen. In recent years, Cai has been having an affair with a neighbor named Zhang Jinguan, which has caused frequent disputes between the couple. The other day, Chunfu and Cai had another conflict, and Cai used a knife to slash at Chunfu. Chunfu reached out and grabbed the knife, injuring his fingers. He then seized the knife and slashed at Cai, injuring her face. She fell to the ground, and he severed her throat, causing her death. Haimen: Yang Wang Commits Suicide Due to Starvation

Yang Kechang, a farmer from Juxing Town Nanli Xu, Fifth District, is in a poor financial situation. Last year, due to a long drought, the cotton and grain harvest was poor, making a living even more difficult. At this time between harvests, the family lacked food and had nothing to cook. The other day (the 20th), Yang's wife, Wang, went to a neighbor's house to borrow rice and wheat but was unsuccessful. Feeling very resentful, she had thoughts of ending her life. That night, she used a razor to slit her throat in the room. By the time Yang realized and tried to save her, her throat had been cut and she had lost too much blood, so the effort was in vain. She died shortly after. Yesterday (the 21st), Yang reported the matter to the county government. After Chen Cheng, the presiding judge, went to investigate, he confirmed that she had committed suicide and ordered the family to collect the body for burial.

Sea Bandits Land and Loot

Tang Zailang, a resident of Maojiagang, Fifth District, is a bamboo craftsman whose earnings are barely enough to make ends meet. Suddenly, at midnight yesterday, seven or eight sea bandits landed in a small boat, each carrying a box gun and flashlight. They went to Tang's house, broke down the door, and grabbed Tang, tying him up with rope and beating him severely. They demanded that he hand over silver dollars, but he refused. They ransacked the house, searching everywhere for over an hour, but found nothing. They then shouted and boarded the boat and left.

American Economic Mission Pays Respects to Mayor Wu Yesterday Morning, Visits Art Exhibition in the Afternoon, and Takes Night Train to Beijing

The eleven members of the American Economic Mission paid their respects to Mayor Wu at the municipal government in the city center at 10:00 yesterday morning. At noon, they attended a banquet hosted by the Sino-American Trade Association at the American Club. Their families attended a luncheon hosted by the American Women's Association. At 3:00 in the afternoon, they visited the Art Exhibition, and at 11:00 in the evening, they took a special train to Beijing to pay respects to the Chinese authorities. In order to expedite the inspection, the previously determined itinerary was changed. A reporter from the Central News Agency has recorded the details as follows:

Paying Respects to the Mayor: At 10:00 yesterday morning, all the members gathered in the reception room on the third floor of the International Hotel. At 10:30, they boarded eight pre-arranged, state-of-the-art cars and set off, accompanied by Guo Bingwen, Zhang Xianglin, Yang Guangxing, Chen Bingzhang, Xia Xiaofang, Wang Erxun, Lu Shou Lian, Wei Xianzhang, and others, along Broadway Road, Yangshupu Road, and Jungong Road to the city center to pay respects to Mayor Wu.

Mayor Welcomes: City government officials invited them to the reception room on the third floor, where Mayor Wu, accompanied by Secretary-General Yu Hongjun, received them. City government secretaries Tang Shixuan and Zhang Tingrong provided refreshments. Mayor Wu expressed his warmest welcome to the mission's leader, Forbes, and wished them a pleasant journey. He also said that the various constructions in the city center, such as the Qiujiang Wharf and the city center railway, would bring Sino-American trade closer together in the future after the success of land-sea transportation.

Praising Construction: They then accompanied the mission to visit the mayor's office, the library, the auditorium, and the model room of the city center's construction, where detailed explanations were given for each room. The mission members expressed great pleasure at the vigorous progress of Shanghai's construction. Finally, they took a group photo on the steps in front of the city government auditorium, shook hands, and parted. The mission members then boarded cars and visited the Zhabei war zone along Jiangwan Road and Baoshan Road, then entered Henan Road and turned into Jiangxi Road, Fuzhou Road, and the American Club to attend a banquet hosted by the Sino-American Trade Association.

Yesterday Afternoon's Reception: The Sino-American Trade Association's banquet was aimed at gathering and connecting with the mission. During the banquet, the association's Fulan District delivered a welcoming speech, and mission leader Forbes thanked them for their hospitality and guidance. Guo Bingwen, Pan Guangjiong, and the president of the American Chamber of Commerce then made brief speeches. The mission members expressed great interest and admiration for these ancient artifacts of Eastern culture. They returned to their residences at 5:00. The mission then took a night train to Beijing at 11:00 last night. Pan Guangjiong and Zhang Xianglin went to see them off. The Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Bureaus specially provided a decorated car and sent staff to provide assistance to show their hospitality. Hou Aichang, representing the entire association, and Tang Dehua, representing the Ministry of Railways, accompanied them. Wang Zhisheng from the reception office also went along to take care of them. The entire group is scheduled to return to Shanghai by China Aviation Corporation Douglas aircraft at 4:00 p.m. on the 25th.

Various Public Banquets: Mayor Wu will host a banquet at the municipal government in the city center at 7:00 p.m. on the 25th, and invitations have already been sent out. At 7:00 p.m. on the 26th, sixteen local organizations will host a public banquet at the International YMCA on Jing'an Temple Road. The reception office has issued over two hundred invitations, including prominent figures in politics, local dignitaries, leaders in industry and commerce, representatives of various organizations, prominent Americans in Shanghai, and the Chinese and Western press. It will be a grand banquet, rarely seen in Shanghai, entirely contracted by Xinghualou, with Chinese cuisine served in a Western style. Western guests will wear formal attire on that day, and Chinese hosts and guests should wear mandarin gowns if they are wearing Chinese dress, and be seated at 7:00 p.m. sharp.

Hua Xigui, Qualified Chinese Pilot from the Far East Aviation School

Hua Xigui (transliteration), a former student of the Hong Kong Far East Aviation Training School, recently passed the Hong Kong government technical examination and obtained a Class C basic pilot's certificate. He is the first Chinese person in Hong Kong's aviation history to obtain this qualification. Mr. Hua enrolled in the school as a mechanic student in 1934. Normally, those who apply for the basic technician examination must prove to the government's aviation affairs officer that they have at least two years of experience in the care of aircraft or aircraft engines, or that they have received two years of training at a government-recognized aviation school, before they are qualified to take the examination. However, because Mr. Hua had previously studied in the mechanics department for five years, this qualification was reduced to one year. China's aviation industry urgently needs trained basic pilots. The efficiency of a country's aviation affairs depends on experts taking care of and maintaining the necessary aviation equipment. The construction of modern aircraft is very complex and requires pilots with in-depth technical expertise to take care of it. The field of aviation mechanics is vast and still awaits scholars to study and develop it. Therefore, the future of trained aircraft mechanics is truly limitless. Currently, there are forty-four people receiving long-term training in the mechanics department at the Far East Aviation School. Their training regulations are the same as those set by the British Aviation Department, and they are committed to creating practical talents. It is hoped that Mr. Hua will be the first of many qualified mechanics to graduate from the Far East Aviation School. Mr. Hua has now been given an aviation position.

Aircraft Repair Factory (Hua Xigui is in the left corner)

National United Telegram Requests Opinions on Goods from Various Regions, Bankruptcy Law and Inspection of Goods for Domestic Sale

The National Federation of Chambers of Commerce of the Republic of China yesterday telegraphed chambers of commerce across the country, saying: To all city chambers of commerce across the country, We hereby notify you that the Legislative Yuan's Civil Law Committee has sent a letter, stating: In order to comply with the Yuan's order, the bankruptcy law has been drafted, and a preliminary draft has now been completed. It has been decided to publicly solicit opinions in order to consider amendments before submitting it to the Yuan for discussion, so as to achieve perfection. We hope that your chamber of commerce will express your opinions and send them to this association by May 10 of this year. Furthermore, the Legislative Yuan's Legal System Committee and Economic Committee jointly sent a letter, stating: The committee is now examining the draft outline of the Inspection of Goods for Domestic Sale, which was submitted by the Yuan for discussion. Regarding the implementation of inspection of goods for domestic sale, the types of goods that should be inspected, the inspection locations, and the collection of inspection fees, etc., please provide detailed information if you have any comments for reference. As each approval is in place, we find the two drafts to be very important. In addition to studying them at this association, we are sending you a copy of the main points of the draft outline of the Inspection of Goods for Domestic Sale. We hope that you will conduct a thorough study of the two drafts and express your opinions directly to the committees of the Legislative Yuan to achieve perfection. Please request the draft bankruptcy law from the Civil Law Committee of the Legislative Yuan. Attachment: Lin Kanghou, Chairman of the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce, respectfully announces, "Attached are the main points of the draft outline of the Inspection of Goods for Domestic Sale:" (1) Situations of various items in Article 1 of the Law on Inspection of Goods for Domestic Sale, which should be implemented again in the inspection of domestic sales to promote their improvement. (2) Goods that have been inspected in accordance with the implementation of the Law on Inspection of Goods, and should also implement domestic sales inspection at the same time, in order to achieve thorough results. (3) Domestic sales inspection is implemented at the collection and distribution markets. (4) The types and locations of goods that should be inspected are stipulated by the Ministry of Industry. (5) Goods that should be inspected should be reported for inspection before the transaction is completed. (6) Goods that should be inspected may be bought and sold in the market after inspection and obtaining a certificate. The validity period of each goods certificate is stipulated by the Ministry of Industry. (7) Inspection of goods for domestic sale should be free of charge. If there are goods for which inspection fees must be charged, the fee should be limited to half of the amount stipulated in Article 7 of the Law on Inspection of Goods.

Banks Release 5 Million Consecutively for Three Days, Solution for a Smooth Passage Through the End of April

Jia Shi News Agency reports that in order to regulate the market, major banks such as China Merchants Bank and Bank of Communications have been actively engaged in interbank collateral loans since the 22nd. As of yesterday, the amount has reached more than 5 million yuan. On the 22nd, the three banks, China Merchants Bank, Bank of Communications, and others, jointly released more than 4 million yuan, of which the Bank of China released the most directly, reaching more than 3 million yuan. Yesterday (23rd), many money shops continued to request loans. In the morning, the three banks still released loans through the Bank of China, about 400,000 to 500,000 yuan. In the afternoon, tens of thousands of yuan were released successively. Therefore, the total amount released in the past two days has exceeded 5 million yuan. The loan method is the same as before, with the three banks announcing the daily interest rate every day. The daily interest rate for the past two days has been 2 jiao. In addition, the real estate deeds used by the money shops when requesting loans may be approved on a case-by-case basis after obtaining certification from the guild if the transfer cannot be completed temporarily. After the implementation of the large-scale loans by the three banks, the general situation has become stable, and it is expected that the number of people requesting loans today will decrease.

Interest on Renewed Loans at the End of April Appropriately Reduced

Regarding the long-term loans issued by various money shops, which will expire at the end of April, amounting to about 40 million yuan, due to the poor business conditions this year, most stores have difficulty clearing inventory, and it is quite difficult to repay the long-term loans, requesting permission to renew them. It is now learned that the money industry, as the banks have agreed to provide current loan to the money industry and maintain the market, the renewal of these loan can be approved, except for a small number of less creditworthy, but the money industry will moderately raise the interest rate by 1 to 1.5 li to compensate. The interest rates for merchants with excellent credit will remain the same.

Continued Increase in Silver Deposits Survey

According to the Central Bank's announcement, the total silver deposits in the city's Chinese and foreign banks last week were 338,626,000 yuan, an increase of 1,471,000 yuan compared to the previous week's 337,155,000 yuan. Of this, Chinese banks accounted for 288,270,000 yuan, and foreign banks accounted for 50,356,000 yuan. Chinese banks continued to increase compared to the previous week, while foreign banks decreased by another 8,000 yuan.

City Chamber of Commerce Requests the Public Works Department to Stop Telephone Rate Hikes and Cancel Tolls for Calls Between Chinese Concessions

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, having received a joint request from various trade associations in the city, such as the restaurant industry, urging negotiations with the Public Works Department to promptly rescind the proposed rate increase by the telephone company to alleviate the merchants' difficulties, specially submitted a report to the municipal government yesterday. Copies were also sent to the Public Works Department of the International Settlement and the Board of Directors of the French Concession for their information. The original text is as follows: "Report for Requesting Matters: On the 23rd of this month, we received a joint letter from the following trade associations in the city: restaurant industry, cotton cloth industry, machine embroidery and dyeing industry, cotton trading houses, local goods industry, iron printing and can manufacturing industry, biscuit, candy, and canned goods industry, silk and satin printing industry, thermos manufacturing industry, Chinese and Western furniture stores, hardware industry, yellow sand and crushed stone industry, forwarding industry, coal industry, sandalwood and longan trading houses, postal transport industry, bamboo industry, cotton ginning industry, cattle and sheep industry, machine-made noodle industry, umbrella industry, egg industry, cold air and ice industry, chemical fertilizer sales industry, enamel industry, glass industry, woolens industry, eyeglasses industry, paint industry, bookstores, electrical silk weaving factories, sausage industry, domestic rubber products industry, refining industry, knitting industry, electrical appliance industry, freight trucking industry, pawnshop industry, etc., stating that 'The telephone bureau is a public utility and should consider the interests of the society and the public, thereby promoting local economic development and expanding its own business. Both parties are closely related and should maintain each other to achieve common prosperity. However, the Shanghai Telephone Company only knows how to seek private gain. Amidst the turbulent economic downturn in the city, it suddenly proposed a telephone rate increase, causing panic and outcry among various industries, yet to this day, the company authorities have not shown any sign of remorse or rescinded the proposal. Merchants from various industries, after much reflection, believe that in addition to the rate increase issue, which should be fought to the death with the support of your esteemed association, there is also the issue of tolls for calls between the Chinese concessions, which has been unresolved for many years. The company's exploitation is increasing day by day, and the suffering of the merchants and the people is deepening. We will further explain this situation to the gentlemen of your esteemed association. The Shanghai Chinese and International Settlements are adjacent to each other, and their business relationships are inseparable. Calls between them should not be subject to additional fees, which would burden the entire commercial sector. Previously, various industries jointly opposed this in newspapers, but the Shanghai Telephone Company has firmly insisted on charging tolls for calls, citing the temporary telephone contract, which stipulates a fee of five cents per call, as an excuse. However, the telephone contract's provision was solely a unilateral claim by the company, and the Chinese authorities repeatedly negotiated for its cancellation without success. To this day, calls between the Chinese concessions not only incur substantial costs but also require manual switching, which is slow, laborious, and costly, severely impacting the future of commerce. Even more appalling is that the company's billing for calls between the Chinese concessions for various businesses is entirely fictitious, without any factual basis. It either reports no calls as calls or underreports calls as more calls, arbitrarily listing them to satisfy its private desires. If questioned, it responds rudely, making it unapproachable. Merchants and people's hard-earned money is not easy to come by. At a time of financial hardship and public distress, how can they bear the additional burden on top of the fixed rental fees to satisfy the company's insatiable demands? Therefore, we are stating the situation. As the dispute over the rate increase remains unresolved, we request that your esteemed association consider the suffering of the people and submit the issue of tolls for calls between the Chinese concessions and the recent telephone rate increase to the Shanghai Municipal Government for resolution. Simultaneously, please have the Public Works Department of the International Settlement forward a message to the Shanghai Telephone Company, urging it to promptly rescind the said toll collection method and the proposed telephone rate increase to alleviate the merchants' difficulties. If the company disregards public opinion and insists on having its way, we implore your esteemed association to identify the objective, persevere to the end, and engage in a long-term struggle with unwavering spirit. In the future, if the situation demands it, we will not hesitate to make sacrifices. We hope that the gentlemen of your esteemed association will vigorously preside over this matter to comfort the long-awaited wishes of the merchants and the people. This will not only be the good fortune of the same industry but also the blessing of the entire citizenry.' After this matter was brought to the association, we, after observing the current social situation, believe that the company's profits last year exceeded six percent, which is unmatched by any other business in these depressed times. It should not extract public funds to enrich itself further. We have twice sent letters to the Public Works Department expressing this view and urging it to prevent the company from raising prices. Furthermore, Chairman Yu of our association attended a meeting of the Public Works Department's Public Utilities Committee and expressed our opposition to the rate increase and strongly condemned the collection of fees per call. In all these situations, we have stated that our association represents the interests of all the merchants in the city. The proposed rate increase by the company must be abandoned. The merchants and the people of the city will not be able to rest easy until this is done. As for the toll of five cents for each call to the Chinese concessions, the measure is particularly inappropriate. The telephone company of the International Settlement and the Shanghai Telephone Bureau have their lines within the same city area and have both adopted automatic switching equipment. Calls between them can be made directly by dialing. Why must there be manual switching, which only burdens citizens with an additional five cents per call? This is truly unreasonable and should be abolished altogether. Based on the aforementioned letter, we hereby submit this document to your esteemed government for review and approval. Please order the Public Utilities Bureau to promptly negotiate with the authorities of the International Settlement to prevent this from happening. This would be in the best interests of the public." (The letters to the Public Works Department, etc., are the same, so they are omitted.)

Overseas Chinese in Siam Hope to Sign a Sino-Siamese Commercial Treaty; Representatives Returning to China to Petition Will Arrive in Shanghai Soon

According to Xin Sheng News Agency, regarding the previous decree issued by the Siamese government to suppress Chinese education, which has recently intensified, with the re-issuance of harsh laws restricting the residence and business of overseas Chinese, the Xin Sheng News Agency reporter has obtained the following information from the Shanghai Chinese United Association:

Newly Revised Harsh Regulations

According to the person in charge of the association, the Chinese Education Regulations enacted by the Siamese government last year were revised once this year and will soon be formally implemented. The content of these regulations almost turns the overseas Chinese in Siam into illiterates. It stipulates that Chinese schools are only allowed to teach Chinese for three hours per week, averaging less than one lesson per day. All textbooks must be in Siamese. What is even harsher is that the Ministry of Education has specially assigned someone to each Chinese school to supervise it, almost completely controlling all school affairs, leaving the principal with only an empty title.

Representatives Petition

Subsequently, any Chinese schools that do not comply will be sealed up. So far, four schools, including Chongshi, Sanmin, Yihua, and Yixin, have been closed in Bangkok. As a result, the relationship between the Siamese and the Chinese is deteriorating day by day. Therefore, after receiving the report, this association has already appealed to the government, requesting prompt negotiations to stop this. The overseas Chinese in Siam have also sent three representatives back to China, who are expected to arrive in Shanghai soon. At that time, this association will also send representatives to Beijing to jointly file an effective petition.

A Treaty Should Be Signed Quickly

Our country and Siam are countries without a treaty, and there has been no commercial treaty signed to date, nor have ambassadors been exchanged. How can our more than two million overseas Chinese in Siam, living under the rule of others, not suffer? Therefore, in addition to passively demanding that our government promptly negotiate to stop these unequal measures against foreigners by the Siamese government, we also actively hope that the government can quickly sign a commercial treaty with the Siamese government so that both can abide by it. It is rumored that Siam's actions are being instigated by a certain country.

The Zhejiang Provincial Cocoon Industry Association Federation recently held a meeting in Shanghai and resolved to request the Bank of China to initiate the formation of a cocoon lending syndicate to lend money to various factories specifically for the purchase of cocoons. Polish Goods Exhibition Postponed to Today Due to Ship's Delayed Arrival Due to Fog

The Polish Ministry of Trade specially dispatched the ship "Dar Pomorza" in January, fully loaded with approximately 10,000 tons of various Polish products. Departing from Gdynia, it passed through the South Sea Islands and Singapore before heading directly to Hong Kong. Along the way, it stopped at various important ports for several days, inviting local people from all walks of life to board the ship for tours and exhibitions. After the exhibition in Hong Kong, it sailed to Shanghai, scheduled to arrive yesterday morning, and the opening ceremony of the Polish Goods Exhibition was to be held on the ship starting yesterday, with a public exhibition for three days. On the 27th, it will sail to Dalian, then to Kobe and Yokohama for exhibitions, before returning to Shanghai to move the samples to the Polish Chamber of Commerce in China for permanent display. However, due to heavy fog at sea in recent days, the ship did not arrive in Shanghai until 5 PM yesterday and was moored at the New Jardine Matheson Wharf in Pudong. Therefore, it has been postponed by one day and will open for public exhibition starting today and until the 27th. On the 28th, it will sail to Dalian. Those who wish to visit can go to the New Customs Wharf and take a free ferry, which departs every half hour. A tea party will also be held on the ship at 4 PM today to welcome business and Chinese and Western press representatives for a visit.
